<h1 class="entry-title penci-entry-title penci-title-">Nyitólap</h1><div class="penci-schema-markup"><span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://hirmagazin.eu/author/nyesteb/">info</a></span><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2024-05-22T06:50:33+02:00">2024-05-22</time><time class="updated" datetime="2026-01-19T14:46:48+01:00">2026-01-19</time></div>															</header>
<div class="penci-entry-content entry-content">
<div  class="hirmag-6bcad1edc345b1cd98dfd6d2e3441394 hirmag-cikkek-elejen" id="hirmag-6bcad1edc345b1cd98dfd6d2e3441394"></div><div class="wpb-content-wrapper"><div class="vc_row wpb_row vc_row_51886553 vc_row-fluid penci-pb-row"><div class="wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-12 penci-col-12"><div class="vc_column-inner wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-12 penci-col-12 "><div class="wpb_wrapper">
<div id="penci_block_26__56263977" class="penci-block-vc penci-block_26 penci__general-meta style-title-1 style-title-left penci-imgtype-landscape penci-link-filter-hidden penci-empty-block-title penci-vc-column-3" data-current="1" data-blockUid="penci_block_26__56263977" >
<div class="penci-block-heading">
</div>
<div id="penci_block_26__56263977block_content" class="penci-block_content">
<div class="penci-block_content__items penci-block-items__1"><div class="penci-block-wrapper-item"><article  class="block26_first_item hentry penci-post-item"><div class="penci_post_thumb"><a class="penci-image-holder  penci-lazy penci-image_has_icon"  data-src="https://hirmagazin.eu/wp-content/uploads/2025/06/rendorsegi-hirek1-668x445.png" data-delay="" href="https://hirmagazin.eu/fokuszban-a-kozbiztonsag-friss-hirek-a-rendorsegtol-31/" title="Fókuszban a közbiztonság – friss hírek a rendőrségtől .."></a></div> <div class="penci_post_content"><h3 class="penci__post-title entry-title"><a href="https://hirmagazin.eu/fokuszban-a-kozbiztonsag-friss-hirek-a-rendorsegtol-31/" title=" Fókuszban a közbiztonság – friss hírek a rendőrségtől ..
